***harmonica.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:harmonica.html>harmonica</a> (20326)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:harmonica.html>harmonica</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">harmonicas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a musical wind instrument with a series of <a href = vnd.unilang:holes.html>holes</a> for the player to blow into, each hole producing a different note</li>
<li>a musical instrument, consisting of a series of hemispherical glasses which, by touching the edges with the dampened finger, give forth the tones.</li>
<li>a toy instrument of <a href = vnd.unilang:strips.html>strips</a> of glass or metal hung on two <a href = vnd.unilang:tapes.html>tapes</a>, and struck with hammers.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">French harp</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">gob iron</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">Mississippi sax</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">mouth harp</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">mouth organ</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">tin sandwich</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:harmonica.html>harmonica</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:muziekinstrument.html>muziekinstrument</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> trekharmonica

<li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:muziekinstrument.html>muziekinstrument</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mondharmonica.html>mondharmonica</a>

***harmonie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:harmonie.html>harmonie</a> (7691)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">harmonia</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">armonie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:harmonie.html>harmonie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">harmonia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἁρμονία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">harmonía</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:harmonie.html>harmonie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:harmonie.html>harmonieën</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:harmonie.html>harmonietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">harmony</span></li>

***harmonium.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:harmonium.html>harmonium</a> (64830)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:harmonium.html>harmonium</a></i>, a term coined by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexandre_Debain" class="extiw" title="w:Alexandre Debain">Alexandre Debain</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:harmonium.html>harmonium</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">harmoniums</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A small keyboard instrument that consists of a series of <a href = vnd.unilang:reed.html>reed</a> pipes, which sound when one of the keys <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> pressed to open a valve that allows air to pass through.
<ul><li><b>1933</b>, George Orwell, <i>Down and Out in Paris and London</i>, Harcourt Brace Jovanivich, page 181:
<dl><dd>They <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> a grave and reverend seignior in a frock coat, a lady sitting at a <a href = vnd.unilang:portable.html>portable</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:harmonium.html>harmonium</a></b>, and a chinless youth toying with a <a href = vnd.unilang:crucifix.html>crucifix</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li>See Wikipedia for differences in usage between US and UK</li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">harpie</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">arpie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">harpie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">harpyia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἅρπυια</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hárpuia</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***harpoen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:harpoen.html>harpoen</a> (25344)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">arpoen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">harpon</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hook, hold-on</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:harpoon.html>harpoon</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Harpune</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:harpoen.html>harpoen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:harpoenen.html>harpoenen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:harpoen.html>harpoentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:harpoon.html>harpoon</a>, short spearlike weapon with tenderhooks thrown at the target, of various sizes and <a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a>, e.g. used for whaling</li>
<li>Some similar <a href = vnd.unilang:weapons.html>weapons</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A figure representing a <a href = vnd.unilang:harpoon.html>harpoon</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">harpoenist</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>

***harridan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:harridan.html>harridan</a> (36047)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps a modification of <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">haridelle</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">old horse, nag</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:harridan.html>harridan</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">harridans</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A vicious and scolding woman, especially an older one.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">shrew</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1848</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Makepeace_Thackeray" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Makepeace Thackeray">William Makepeace Thackeray</a>, <i>Vanity Fair</i>, Chapter 13:
<dl><dd>Why <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that tattling old <b><a href = vnd.unilang:harridan.html>harridan</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:peggy.html>Peggy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>'Dowd, to make free with my name at her d—d supper-table, and advertise my engagement <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the three kingdoms?</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***harry.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:harry.html>harry</a> (984)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">herien</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">harien</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walloon_language" class="extiw" title="w:Walloon language">Walloon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="wa">hairyî</i>, old French <i class="Latn mention" lang="wa">hairier</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="wa">harier</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">herġian</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*harjōną</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">ferheerje</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">verheeren</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:harry.html>harry</a>, devastate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">härja</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ravage, <a href = vnd.unilang:harry.html>harry</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*harjaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">army</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">here</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">hear</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heer.html>heer</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:heer.html>Heer</a></i>), from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*koryos</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Irish">Middle Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="mga">cuire</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">army</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">kãrias</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">army; war</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">кара</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:kara.html>kara</a></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">strife</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κοίρανος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">koíranos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">chief, commander</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Persian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Persian">Old Persian</a></span> <small>[script needed]</small> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="peo-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kāra</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">army</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>). More at <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">here</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">army</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:harry.html>harry</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">harries</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">harrying</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">harried</b>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>To plunder, pillage, assault.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Shakespeare to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>To make repeated attacks on an enemy.
<ul><li><b>1906</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alfred_Noyes" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alfred Noyes">Alfred Noyes</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Highwayman_(Noyes)" class="extiw" title="wikisource:The Highwayman (Noyes)">The Highwayman</a></i>:
<dl><dd>"One kiss, my <a href = vnd.unilang:bonny.html>bonny</a> sweetheart, I'm after a prize to-night,</dd>
<dd>But I shall be back with the yellow gold before the morning light;</dd>
<dd>Yet, if they press <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> sharply, and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:harry.html>harry</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> through the day,</dd>
<dd>Then look for <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> by moonlight,</dd>
<dd>Watch for <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> by moonlight,</dd>
<dd>I'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> come to <a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a> by moonlight, though Hell should <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a> the way."</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>To strip, lay waste, ravage.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Washington Irving and provide title, author's full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:harry.html>harry</a></b> this beautiful region</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by J. Burroughs and provide title, author's full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>A red squirrel <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <b>harried</b> the nest of a wood thrush.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>To harass, bother or distress with demands, threats, or criticism.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> October 23,  Becky Ashton,  “QPR 1 – 0 Chelsea”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/BBC_Sport" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:BBC Sport">BBC Sport</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/football/eng_prem/15325522.stm">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Chelsea also struggled to keep possession as QPR <b>harried</b> and chased at every opportunity, giving their opponents no time on the ball.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b> July 5,  <a href = vnd.unilang:sam.html>Sam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:borden.html>Borden</a>,  “For bellicose Brazil, payback <a href = vnd.unilang:carries.html>carries</a> heavy price: Loss of Neymar  | <i>International New York Times</i> version: Brazil and referee share some blame for Neymar's injury: Spaniard's failure to curb early pattern of fouls <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> seen as major factor (7 July 2014, p. 13) | ”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_New_York_Times" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The New York Times">The New York Times</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2014/07/06/sports/worldcup/for-bellicose-brazil-payback-carries-heavy-price-loss-of-neymar.html">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The Colombians' ire <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> raised <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> more 10 minutes <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> when the referee showed a yellow card to  | James |  Rodríguez  – who <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> apoplectic at the decision – for an innocuous trip that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>, as Rodríguez vociferously pointed out with multiple hand gestures, a first offense compared with Fernandinho's <b>harrying</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***hart.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hart.html>hart</a> (483)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">herte</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:harte.html>harte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">herta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hertô</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱḗr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hart.html>hart</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:harten.html>harten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hartje.html>hartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>heart, main muscle pumping blood through the body:</li>
<li>The center point or zone of an object, image etc.</li>
<li>The core or essence of some thing, reasoning etc.</li>
<li>Compassionate or similar <a href = vnd.unilang:feelings.html>feelings</a></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hart.html>hart</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:harten.html>harten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hartje.html>hartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_dialects" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch dialects">Northern</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Archaic form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hert.html>hert</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">deer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>.</li></ol>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***hartslag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hartslag.html>hartslag</a> (4366)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hart.html>hart</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">heart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slag.html>slag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hit, beat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***hatchet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hatchet.html>hatchet</a> (82897)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">hachet</i>, a borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">hachete</i>, diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">hache</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">axe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*hapja</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*happija</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hapjō</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*habjō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knife</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kop-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to strike, to beat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">happa</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">heppa</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">habba</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:reaper.html>reaper</a>, sickle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:hippe.html>Hippe</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">billhook</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hatchet.html>hatchet</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hatchets</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A small light axe with a short handle; a <a href = vnd.unilang:tomahawk.html>tomahawk</a>.
<ul><li><b>1855</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_Wadsworth_Longfellow" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry Wadsworth Longfellow"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Wadsworth Longfellow</a>, <i>The Song of Hiawatha</i>
<dl><dd>Buried <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the bloody <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hatchet.html>hatchet</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hatchet.html>hatchet</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">hatchets</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hatcheting</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hatchetting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hatcheted</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hatchetted</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cut with a <a href = vnd.unilang:hatchet.html>hatchet</a>.</li></ol>
</body>

***have.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> have (10)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b>have</b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:overgankelijk.html>overgankelijk</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></li>
<li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">hulpwerkwoord</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></li>
<li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">hulpwerkwoord</span> (to + infinitief) <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a>
<dl><dd>«I <b>have</b> to go.»
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a>.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>

***haver.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:haver.html>haver</a> (25343)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">havere</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*havara</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*habrô</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hafri</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:haver.html>haver</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">habaro</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haver.html>haver</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haver.html>havertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>any wild species or cultivar of the genus <i>Avena</i></li>
<li>in particular, <i>Avena <a href = vnd.unilang:sativa.html>sativa</a></i>, the cereal oats, notably fed to <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>horses</a></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haver.html>haver</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">haveren</i></span></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">first-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">haveren</i></span></li></ol>

<ul><li>havermoutpap</li></ul>

***havik.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:havik.html>havik</a> (13385)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">havic</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*havuk</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*habukaz</i>, probably ultimately derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*keh₂p-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seize</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Haavk</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Habicht</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">hauk</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hawk</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">hök</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">hauk</i>. The political sense derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hawk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:havik.html>havik</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haviken.html>haviken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:havik.html>havikje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A hawk, a small bird of the family Accipitridae, especially of the genus <i>Accipiter</i>.</li>
<li>A northern goshawk, <i>Accipiter gentilis</i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A hawk, someone with aggressive or extreme views in (foreign) politics.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:duif.html>duif</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:havik.html>havik</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:vogels.html>vogels</a>)</span> <a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Accipiter_gentilis" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Accipiter gentilis"><span style="color:green;"><i>Accipiter gentilis</i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" />, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roofvogel.html>roofvogel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kleine.html>kleine</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoogdieren.html>zoogdieren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vogels.html>vogels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaagt.html>jaagt</a></li>

***haw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a> (49382)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Imitative
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>An imitation of laughter, often used to express scorn or disbelief. Often doubled or tripled (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a></i> or <i><a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a></i>).
<dl><dd><i>You think that song <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> good? <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>Haw</a>!</b></i></dd></dl></li>
<li>An intermission or hesitation of speech, with a sound somewhat like "<a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a>"; the sound so made.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Congreve and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>Hums or <b>haws</b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">an imitation of laughter</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> In the US, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> (it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> more used in the past), with <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ha.html>ha</a></i> being more common.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">haws</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hawing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hawed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a>, in speaking, with a sound like <i><a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a></i>; to speak with interruption and hesitation.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">hawe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">haga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">enclosure, hedge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hagô</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">haach</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haag.html>haag</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:hag.html>Hag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hedged farmland</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kagʰom</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">cae</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hedge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">caulae</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sheepfold, enclosure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cohum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">strap between plowbeam and yoke</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кош</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">koš</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:tent.html>tent</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">коша́ра</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">košára</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sheepfold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">कक्ष</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kakṣa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">curtain wall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kagʰ-</i> 'to catch, grasp' (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">cau</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to clasp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language">Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq"><a href = vnd.unilang:kam.html>kam</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq"><a href = vnd.unilang:ke.html>ke</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to have, hold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">haws</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Fruit of the hawthorn.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">hawthorn berry</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A hedge.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection_2">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>An instruction for a horse or other animal to turn towards the driver, typically left (See gee).</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">haws</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hawing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hawed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of an animal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To turn towards the driver, typically to the left.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">This horse <a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>won</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a></b> when I tell him to.</i></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">gee</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>To cause (an animal) to turn left.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">You may have to go to the front of the pack and physically <b><a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a></b> the lead dog.</i></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">gee</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Uncertain.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:haw.html>haw</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">haws</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The third eyelid, or nictitating membrane.</li>
<li>A disease of the nictitating membrane.</li></ol>

***hawk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> hawk (6877)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b>hawk</b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:vogels.html>vogels</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:havik.html>havik</a></li>

***hawke.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hawke.html>hawke</a> (60750)</h1><br></body> 
***hawker.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hawker.html>hawker</a> (105662)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">hoker</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hawker.html>hawker</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hawkers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A peddler, huckster, who travels about to sell easily transportable goods.</li>
<li>Any <a href = vnd.unilang:dragonfly.html>dragonfly</a> of the family Aeshnidae; a darner.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hawk</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hawker.html>hawker</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hawkers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Someone who breeds and <a href = vnd.unilang:trains.html>trains</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hawks.html>hawks</a> and other <a href = vnd.unilang:falcons.html>falcons</a>; a falconer.</li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hazelnoot.html>hazelnoot</a> (45384)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hazel.html>hazel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hazel.html>hazel</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:noot.html>noot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:nut.html>nut</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hazelnoot.html>hazelnoot</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hazelnoten.html>hazelnoten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hazelnoot.html>hazelnootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:hazel.html>hazel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nut.html>nut</a></li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:hazel.html>hazel</a>, a <a href = vnd.unilang:hazel.html>hazel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nut.html>nut</a> tree or shrub; tree of the genus <i>Corylus</i>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hazel.html>hazel</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">hazelaar</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***heard.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> (105655)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*harduz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kert-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kret-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">strong; powerful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">herd</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">hard</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:hart.html>hart</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:hart.html>hart</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">harðr</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌷𐌰𐍂𐌳𐌿𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hardus</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latinx headword" lang="ang"><a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>hard, harsh, austere, severe, rigorous, stern, stubborn, firm, hardy, <a href = vnd.unilang:brave.html>brave</a></li></ol>
